  The management is now bothered that if the faculty members also join the strike, there will be a severe problem. Therefore, three members of the management suggested one course of action each to solve this problem.
  Mr. Bell: The faculty members should be persuaded not to go on strike.

Based on the above, decide which of the suggested courses of action should be logically pursued?

Question 4
Privacy at the workplace and a good working environment lead to higher productivity in an organisation. ‘Egoless’ and ‘Bossism’ free environment is the best suitable for employees, and also, the customer can be given the best services. 
 Mr. Bean joined a renowned organisation that provides question banks to its clients. The company provides questions on Maths, Reasoning, Data Interpretation, Verbal Ability and General Awareness. As Mr. Bean is dealing with General awareness, he needs to read a lot and hence, required a noise-free and disturbance-free environment. So, he wrote to the director, “If you want timely completion of work, provide independent cabin”. 
 What is the assumption(s) taken by Mr. Bean? 
I. There are enough cabins. 
II. Others’ presence hinders the timely completion of work. 
Options:
A:
only I 
B:
only II 
C:
both I and II 
D:
neither I nor II 
Question 5
A student, who has passed his higher secondary examination, has many options of the universities from where he can be graduated. But, the syllabus of all universities is different, and the difference is significant. The syllabus is very much updated for some universities, while many subjects that are not relevant in the current scenario are still there in the syllabus of some universities. 
 Prof. Brad told his three students to give an argument on “should there be a common curriculum for a particular degree course in all the universities across a country?” The arguments presented by three students, John, David and Johnny, were noted. 
 John: Yes, this will bring uniformity in the degrees offered by various universities. 
David: No, this is practically not possible, and there is no need for this. 
Johnny: No. doing this will be a wastage of a lot of money and workforce. 
 Based on the above arguments, choose the correct option. 
Options:
A:
Only John’s argument is strong 
B:
Only David’s argument is strong 
C:
Only Johnny’s argument is strong 
D:
None of the arguments is strong
